Γòæ  ≡ƒö┤ CRITICAL VIOLATION
Γòæ  Rule  : FSL-001
Γòæ  File  : lib/core/providers/firebase_providers.dart:24
Γòæ  Issue : StreamProvider.family declared without autoDispose
Γòæ  Code  : StreamProvider.family<DocumentSnapshot<Map<String, dynamic>>?, String>((
Γòæ  Fix   : Change to StreamProvider.autoDispose.family<...>. Per-user/per-id StreamProviders MUST autoDispose ΓÇö without it, stale listeners accumulate as users navigate between rooms/profiles. Exceptions: auth, presence heartbeat, notification badge (explicitly documented).

Γòæ  ≡ƒö┤ CRITICAL VIOLATION
Γòæ  Rule  : FSL-002
Γòæ  File  : lib/features/auth/providers/admin_provider.dart:19
Γòæ  Issue : Unbounded .snapshots() ΓÇö no .limit() within 10 lines. Unbounded queries cause runaway Firestore read costs at scale.
Γòæ  Code  : .snapshots()
Γòæ  Fix   : Add .limit(N) before .snapshots(): feeds/messages/notifications ΓåÆ .limit(50), social graphs/friend lists ΓåÆ .limit(100). QUERY_BOUNDS_RULE: no unbounded .snapshots() permitted.
